#TLSTATUS File is edited by RaurosFalls 12/09/14
# みかんフェラチオ調教まとめ
# For Mikan fellatio training
label	training_mikan_fellatio
sel=0

#SCRIPT IGNORE
select_icon_init
#SCRIPT IGNORE END

if _COLOR=228 then sel=0	#口
if _COLOR=86  then sel=1	#顔

skip_untranslated_training=0
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1=0 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_01
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1=1 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_02
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1=2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_03
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1>2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_04

if skip_untranslated_training=1 then return
t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1=t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1+1

#SCRIPT IGNORE
activity_count=t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
gosub training_stat_handle_oral
@training_mikan_load
return
#SCRIPT SKIP JAPANESE LINES 3
add_karada=add_karada+3*t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
add_kokoro=add_kokoro+5*t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
add_miryoku=add_miryoku+10*t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
#SCRIPT IGNORE END

tairyoku=tairyoku-30*t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
seishin=seishin-40*t_mikan_fellatio_cnt1
lifebar_setauto	life_tairyoku,tairyoku
lifebar_setauto	life_seishin,seishin

@training_mikan_load

return

macro	t_mikan_fera_sub
if sel=1 then goto training_mikan_fellatio_mouth
if sel=0 then goto training_mikan_fellatio_face

#口の中に射精する
label	training_mikan_fellatio_mouth
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2=0 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_a01
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2=1 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_a02
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2=2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_a03
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2>2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_a04
t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2=t_mikan_fellatio_cnt2+1

goto	training_mikan_fellatio_skip
#顔に射精する
label	training_mikan_fellatio_face
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3=0 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_b01
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3=1 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_b02
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3=2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_b03
if t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3>2 then gosub training_mikan_fellatio_b04
t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3=t_mikan_fellatio_cnt3+1
label	training_mikan_fellatio_skip

endm
